\DoxyCodeLine{786   \textcolor{comment}{// Filling an object's fields can cause GCs and heap walks, so this object has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{787   \textcolor{comment}{// to be in a 'sufficiently initialised' state by the time the next allocation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{788   \textcolor{comment}{// can happen. For this to be the case, the object is carefully deserialized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{789   \textcolor{comment}{// as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{790   \textcolor{comment}{//   * The space for the object is allocated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{791   \textcolor{comment}{//   * The map is set on the object so that the GC knows what type the object}}
\DoxyCodeLine{792   \textcolor{comment}{//     has.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{793   \textcolor{comment}{//   * The rest of the object is filled with a fixed Smi value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{794   \textcolor{comment}{//     -\/ This is a Smi so that tagged fields become initialized to a valid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{795   \textcolor{comment}{//       tagged value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{796   \textcolor{comment}{//     -\/ It's a fixed value, "{}Smi::uninitialized\_deserialization\_value()"{}, so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{797   \textcolor{comment}{//       that we can DCHECK for it when reading objects that are assumed to be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{798   \textcolor{comment}{//       partially initialized objects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{799   \textcolor{comment}{//   * The fields of the object are deserialized in order, under the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{800   \textcolor{comment}{//     assumption that objects are laid out in such a way that any fields}}
\DoxyCodeLine{801   \textcolor{comment}{//     required for object iteration (e.g. length fields) are deserialized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{802   \textcolor{comment}{//     before fields with objects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{803   \textcolor{comment}{//     -\/ We ensure this is the case by DCHECKing on object allocation that the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{804   \textcolor{comment}{//       previously allocated object has a valid size (see `Allocate`).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{805 }
